## 7. Upload Execution Plan

### Phase 1: Create Categories in Sanity
- Write a Node.js script (`scripts/seed-categories.ts`) using Sanity client
- Create all 61 categories with `name` and `order` fields
- Store created document IDs for reference

### Phase 2: Upload Product Images to Sanity
- Write a script (`scripts/upload-images.ts`) that:
  - Reads all matchable images from `product-files/viswas products/`
  - Uploads each to Sanity as an asset using `client.assets.upload()`
  - For duplicate images, upload primary version only
  - Skips ambiguous images (IMG-*, Screenshot-*, hash-named files)
  - Saves mapping: `{ filename -> sanityAssetId }` to a JSON file

### Phase 3: Create Products in Sanity
- Write a script (`scripts/seed-products.ts`) that:
  - Reads product data and category mappings
  - For each product: generates slug from name, maps to category reference
  - Where image exists, attaches uploaded image asset
  - Where no image, leaves image field empty
  - Uses batch creation for efficiency

### Phase 4: Review & Manual Cleanup
- Manually review in Sanity Studio (`/studio`)
- Assign ambiguous images to correct products
- Choose best image from duplicates
- Add missing product details (unit, badge, etc.)
